26/01/16 16:44:17  null            acc.zip(component) { a, b -> (a.toInt() xor b.toInt()).toByte() }.toByteArray()

26/01/16 16:44:17  null    ): HsmCommandResult {
26/01/16 16:44:17  null        val keySize = when (algorithm) {
26/01/16 16:44:17  null            CipherAlgorithm.DES -> 8
26/01/16 16:44:17  null            CipherAlgorithm.TRIPLE_DES -> when (keyLength) {
26/01/16 16:44:17  null                KeyLength.SINGLE -> 8

26/01/16 16:44:18  null        var currentKey = initialKey.copyOf()

26/01/16 16:44:18  null                ((counterBytes[1].toInt() and 0xFF) shl 8) or
26/01/16 16:44:18  null                (counterBytes[2].toInt() and 0xFF)
26/01/16 16:44:18  null

26/01/16 16:44:18  nullAuditEntry(timestamp=2026-01-16T16:44:18.922527, entryType=HOST_COMMAND, command=    , user=CONSOLE, lmkId=, result=FAILED, details=Unknown command:   )
